			i{int} {i}  := 0

				articulations_note_off(i{int} {i} , EVENT_NOTE{int} {EVENT_NOTE} ){UserDefined, None}

			end while
			wait_or_zero(NOTE_SELECTION_TIME{int} {NOTE_SELECTION_TIME}  * 1000){UserDefined, None}
			i{int} {i}  := 0
			while(i{int} {i}  <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} {NUM_INSTRUMENTS}  - 1))

		end if
	end if
end on

on controller{thread-unsafe}
	ignore_controller{Builtin, None}
	declare local controller_value : int {thread-unsafe} := CC[CC_NUM{int} {CC_NUM} ]{int} {CC}  {Reuses: 0}
	if(CC_NUM{int} {CC_NUM}  = 1)
		buffer_modwheel_animation(CC[1]{int} {CC} ){UserDefined, None}
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_modwheel_slider{int} {sli_modwheel_slider} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , CC[1]{int} {CC} ){Builtin, None}
	end if
	if(CC_NUM{int} {CC_NUM}  = 64)
		if(CC[64]{int} {CC}  > 63)
			sustain_pedal_actual{int} {sustain_pedal_actual}  := ON{int} {ON} 
		else
			sustain_pedal_actual{int} {sustain_pedal_actual}  := OFF{int} {OFF} 
			sustain_pedal{int} {sustain_pedal}  := OFF{int} {OFF} 
			i{int} {i}  := nki_range[0]{int} {nki_range} 
			while(i{int} {i}  <= nki_range[1]{int} {nki_range} ) 
				if(pressed_keys[i{int} {i} ]{int} {pressed_keys}  = - 1)
					ii{int} {ii}  := 0
					while(ii{int} {ii}  <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} {NUM_INSTRUMENTS}  - 1)) 
						if(pressed_notes_per_instrument[ii{int} {ii} , i{int} {i} ]{int} {pressed_notes_per_instrument}  = ON{int} {ON} )
							articulations_note_off(ii{int} {ii} , i{int} {i} ){UserDefined, None}
						end if
						inc(ii{int} {ii} ){Builtin, None}
					end while
					set_key_pressed(i{int} {i} , 0){Builtin, None}
				end if
				inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
	end if
	wait_or_zero((lookahead{int} {lookahead}  * 1000) * use_constant_delay{int} {use_constant_delay} ){UserDefined, None}
	sustain_pedal{int} {sustain_pedal}  := sustain_pedal_actual{int} {sustain_pedal_actual} 
	if(CC_NUM{int} {CC_NUM}  = 1)
		set_modulation_position(0, controller_value{int} {controller_value} ){UserDefined, None}

	end if
end on

on ui_control(xy_center_circles{real[]} {xy_center_circles} ){thread-unsafe}
	cc_cb_id{int} {cc_cb_id}  := NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} {NI_CALLBACK_ID} 
	declare local angle : real {thread-unsafe} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local value : int {thread-unsafe} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local distance : real {thread-unsafe} {Reuses: 0}
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} {NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE}  = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN{int} {NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_LEFT_BUTTON_DOWN} )
		center_circle_distance(distance{real} {distance} , xy_center_circles[0]{real} {xy_center_circles} , xy_center_circles[1]{real} {xy_center_circles} ){UserDefined, None}
		center_circle_angle(angle{real} {angle} , xy_center_circles[0]{real} {xy_center_circles} , xy_center_circles[1]{real} {xy_center_circles} ){UserDefined, None}
		angle_to_value(value{int} {value} , angle{real} {angle} , 0.7, (NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI}  * 2) - 0.7){UserDefined, None}
		if((distance{real} {distance}  >= 0.32) and (distance{real} {distance}  < 0.36))
			selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation}  := 0
		else
			if((distance{real} {distance}  >= 0.36) and (distance{real} {distance}  < 0.4))
				selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation}  := 1
			else
				if((distance{real} {distance}  >= 0.4) and (distance{real} {distance}  < 0.44))
					selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation}  := 2
				else
					if((distance{real} {distance}  >= 0.44) and (distance{real} {distance}  < 0.48))
						selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation}  := 3
					end if
				end if
			end if
		end if
		if(abs(value{int} {value}  - loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} , selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_start} ){Builtin, None} < 10)

				selected_circle_end{int} {selected_circle_end}  := 1
			else
				selected_circle_end{int} {selected_circle_end}  := - 1
			end if
		end if
		call update_subarticulation_selection{UserDefined, None}
	end if
	if(NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE{int} {NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE}  = NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DRAG{int} {NI_MOUSE_EVENT_TYPE_DRAG} )
		wait(10000){Builtin, None}
		if((cc_cb_id{int} {cc_cb_id}  = NI_CALLBACK_ID{int} {NI_CALLBACK_ID} ) and (selected_circle_end{int} {selected_circle_end}  # - 1))
			center_circle_angle(angle{real} {angle} , xy_center_circles[0]{real} {xy_center_circles} , xy_center_circles[1]{real} {xy_center_circles} ){UserDefined, None}
			angle_to_value(value{int} {value} , angle{real} {angle} , 0.7, (NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI}  * 2) - 0.7){UserDefined, None}
			if(selected_circle_end{int} {selected_circle_end}  = 0)
				if(value{int} {value}  < ((loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} , selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_end}  - loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} , selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_fade_out} ) - loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} , selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_fade_in} ))
					loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} , selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_start}  := value{int} {value} 
				end if
			else
				if(selected_circle_end{int} {selected_circle_end}  = 1)
					if(value{int} {value}  > ((loaded_subarticulations_start[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} , selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_start}  + loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} , selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_fade_in} ) + loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} , selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_fade_out} ))
						loaded_subarticulations_end[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} , selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_end}  := value{int} {value} 
					end if
				end if
			end if
			call update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, None}
			call update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, None}
		end if
	end if
end on

function update_purge{restricted}
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local ii : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local iii : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local subarticulation_is_loaded[512] : int[] := [0] {Reuses: 0}
	i{int} {i}  := 0
	while(i{int} {i}  <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} {NUM_INSTRUMENTS}  - 1)) 
		ii{int} {ii}  := 0
		while(ii{int} {ii}  <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} {NUM_KEYSWITCHES}  - 1)) 
			iii{int} {iii}  := 0
			while(iii{int} {iii}  <= (4 - 1)) 
				if(loaded_subarticulations[i{int} {i} , ii{int} {ii} , iii{int} {iii} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations}  # - 1)
					subarticulation_is_loaded[loaded_subarticulations[i{int} {i} , ii{int} {ii} , iii{int} {iii} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulation_is_loaded}  := subarticulation_is_loaded[loaded_subarticulations[i{int} {i} , ii{int} {ii} , iii{int} {iii} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulation_is_loaded}  + keyswitch_purge_states[i{int} {i} , ii{int} {ii} ]{int} {keyswitch_purge_states} 
				end if
				inc(iii{int} {iii} ){Builtin, None}
			end while
			inc(ii{int} {ii} ){Builtin, None}
		end while
		inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	i{int} {i}  := 0
	while(i{int} {i}  <= (NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS{int} {NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS}  - 1)) 
		if(subarticulations_group_idx[subarticulations_ids_positions[i{int} {i} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_group_idx}  # NI_NOT_FOUND{int} {NI_NOT_FOUND} )
			if(subarticulation_is_loaded[i{int} {i} ]{int} {subarticulation_is_loaded}  = 0)
				subarticulation_purge(i{int} {i} , OFF{int} {OFF} ){UserDefined, None}
			end if
		end if
		inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	i{int} {i}  := 0
	while(i{int} {i}  <= (NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS{int} {NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS}  - 1)) 
		if(subarticulations_group_idx[subarticulations_ids_positions[i{int} {i} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_group_idx}  # NI_NOT_FOUND{int} {NI_NOT_FOUND} )
			if(subarticulation_is_loaded[i{int} {i} ]{int} {subarticulation_is_loaded}  > 0)
				message("PURGE: Enable " & i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
				subarticulation_purge(i{int} {i} , ON{int} {ON} ){UserDefined, None}
			end if
		end if
		inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function sh_right_safe(val0 : int, pos0 : int)
	return ((sh_right(val0{int} {val0} , 31){Builtin, None} .and. (1 * sh_left(1, 31 - pos0{int} {pos0} ){Builtin, None})) .or. sh_right(val0{int} {val0}  .and. 2147483647, pos0{int} {pos0} ){Builtin, None})
end function

function is_in_range(value0 : int, a0 : int, b0 : int)
	return (1 + (sh_right(b0{int} {b0}  - value0{int} {value0} , 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(value0{int} {value0}  - a0{int} {a0} , 31){Builtin, None}))
end function

function swap(a1 : int, b1 : int)
	a1{int} {a1}  := a1{int} {a1}  .xor. b1{int} {b1} 
	b1{int} {b1}  := b1{int} {b1}  .xor. a1{int} {a1} 
	a1{int} {a1}  := a1{int} {a1}  .xor. b1{int} {b1} 
end function

function gt(a2 : int, b2 : int)
	return (- sh_right(b2{int} {b2}  - a2{int} {a2} , 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function ge(a3 : int, b3 : int)
	return (sh_right(a3{int} {a3}  - b3{int} {b3} , 31){Builtin, None} + 1)
end function

function eq(a4 : int, b4 : int)
	return (- sh_right(abs(a4{int} {a4}  - b4{int} {b4} ){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function lt(a5 : int, b5 : int)
	return (- sh_right(a5{int} {a5}  - b5{int} {b5} , 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function le(a6 : int, b6 : int)
	return (1 + sh_right(b6{int} {b6}  - a6{int} {a6} , 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function ne(x0 : int)
	return (abs(sh_right(abs(x0{int} {x0} ){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function neg(x1 : int)
	return (- sh_right(x1{int} {x1} , 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function bool(x2 : int)
	return (1 + sh_right(abs(x2{int} {x2} ){Builtin, None} - 1, 31){Builtin, None})
end function

function sign(x3 : int)
	return (sh_right(x3{int} {x3} , 31){Builtin, None} .or. 1)
end function

function sign3(x4 : int)
	return (sign(x4{int} {x4} ){UserDefined, None} .and. - bool(x4{int} {x4} ){UserDefined, None})
end function

function bitlist.load(bit_list0 : unknown, val1 : unknown)
	bit_list0{unknown} {bit_list0}  := val1{unknown} {val1} 
end function

function scale.range(input0 : number, currentMin0 : number, currentMax0 : number, scaleToMin0 : number, scaleToMax0 : number)
	return ((((input0{number} {input0}  - currentMin0{number} {currentMin0} ) * (scaleToMax0{number} {scaleToMax0}  - scaleToMin0{number} {scaleToMin0} )) / (currentMax0{number} {currentMax0}  - currentMin0{number} {currentMin0} )) + scaleToMin0{number} {scaleToMin0} )
end function

function scale.range.real(input1 : int, currentMin1 : real, currentMax1 : real, scaleToMin1 : real, scaleToMax1 : real)
	return (real_to_int((((int_to_real(input1{int} {input1} ){Builtin, None} - currentMin1{real} {currentMin1} ) * (scaleToMax1{real} {scaleToMax1}  - scaleToMin1{real} {scaleToMin1} )) / (currentMax1{real} {currentMax1}  - currentMin1{real} {currentMin1} )) + scaleToMin1{real} {scaleToMin1} ){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.range.slider(input2 : real, scaleToMin2 : real, scaleToMax2 : number)
	return (real_to_int(((input2{real} {input2}  * (scaleToMax2{number} {scaleToMax2}  - scaleToMin2{real} {scaleToMin2} )) / 1e+06) + scaleToMin2{real} {scaleToMin2} ){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.slider(input3 : int, scaleToMin3 : real, scaleToMax3 : real)
	return (real_to_int(((int_to_real(input3{int} {input3} ){Builtin, None} * (scaleToMax3{real} {scaleToMax3}  - scaleToMin3{real} {scaleToMin3} )) / 1e+06) + scaleToMin3{real} {scaleToMin3} ){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.range.log(input4 : number, currentMin2 : number, currentMax2 : number, scaleToMin4 : real, scaleToMax4 : real)
	return (pow(10, (log(scaleToMin4{real} {scaleToMin4} ){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None}) + (((input4{number} {input4}  - currentMin2{number} {currentMin2} ) / (currentMax2{number} {currentMax2}  - currentMin2{number} {currentMin2} )) * ((log(scaleToMax4{real} {scaleToMax4} ){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None}) - (log(scaleToMin4{real} {scaleToMin4} ){Builtin, None} / log(10){Builtin, None})))){Builtin, None})
end function

function scale.clamp.to(input5 : int, fromMin0 : int, fromMax0 : int, toMin0 : int, toMax0 : int)
	return (real_to_int(scale.range(int_to_real(((input5{int} {input5}  * (1 + (sh_right(fromMax0{int} {fromMax0}  - input5{int} {input5} , 31){Builtin, None} .or. sh_right(input5{int} {input5}  - fromMin0{int} {fromMin0} , 31){Builtin, None}))) - (fromMin0{int} {fromMin0}  * sh_right(input5{int} {input5}  - fromMin0{int} {fromMin0} , 31){Builtin, None})) - (fromMax0{int} {fromMax0}  * sh_right(fromMax0{int} {fromMax0}  - input5{int} {input5} , 31){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(fromMin0{int} {fromMin0} ){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(fromMax0{int} {fromMax0} ){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(toMin0{int} {toMin0} ){Builtin, None}, int_to_real(toMax0{int} {toMax0} ){Builtin, None}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function isBitSet(x7 : int, pos3 : int)
	return (sh_right(x7{int} {x7} , pos3{int} {pos3} ){Builtin, None} .and. 1)
end function

function set_bit(x8 : int, pos4 : int)
	return (x8{int} {x8}  .or. sh_left(1, pos4{int} {pos4} ){Builtin, None})
end function

function clear_bit(x9 : int, pos5 : int)
	return (x9{int} {x9}  .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos5{int} {pos5} ){Builtin, None})
end function

function flip_bit(x10 : int, pos6 : int)
	return (.not. (.not. (x10{int} {x10}  .and. .not. (x10{int} {x10}  .and. sh_left(1, pos6{int} {pos6} ){Builtin, None})) .and. .not. (sh_left(1, pos6{int} {pos6} ){Builtin, None} .and. .not. (x10{int} {x10}  .and. sh_left(1, pos6{int} {pos6} ){Builtin, None}))))
end function

function modify_bit(x11 : int, pos7 : int, state0 : int)
	return (.not. (.not. ((x11{int} {x11}  .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos7{int} {pos7} ){Builtin, None}) .and. .not. ((x11{int} {x11}  .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos7{int} {pos7} ){Builtin, None}) .and. (- state0{int} {state0}  .and. sh_left(1, pos7{int} {pos7} ){Builtin, None}))) .and. .not. ((- state0{int} {state0}  .and. sh_left(1, pos7{int} {pos7} ){Builtin, None}) .and. .not. ((x11{int} {x11}  .and. .not. sh_left(1, pos7{int} {pos7} ){Builtin, None}) .and. (- state0{int} {state0}  .and. sh_left(1, pos7{int} {pos7} ){Builtin, None})))))

function decimal.to.binary(input6 : int, output_array0 : number[])

function update_instrument_range(instrument1 : int)
	declare local lowest : int := 128 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local highest : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local ks : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local s : int {Reuses: 0}
	ks{int} {ks}  := 0
	while(ks{int} {ks}  <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} {NUM_KEYSWITCHES}  - 1)) 
		if(keyswitch_states[instrument1{int} {instrument1} , ks{int} {ks} ]{int} {keyswitch_states}  = TRUE{int} {TRUE} )
			s{int} {s}  := 0
			while(s{int} {s}  <= (4 - 1)) 
				if(loaded_subarticulations[instrument1{int} {instrument1} , ks{int} {ks} , s{int} {s} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations}  >= 0)
					if(subarticulations_range_lower[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument1{int} {instrument1} , ks{int} {ks} , s{int} {s} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_lower}  < lowest{int} {lowest} )
						lowest{int} {lowest}  := subarticulations_range_lower[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument1{int} {instrument1} , ks{int} {ks} , s{int} {s} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_lower} 
					end if
					if(subarticulations_range_upper[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument1{int} {instrument1} , ks{int} {ks} , s{int} {s} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_upper}  > highest{int} {highest} )
						highest{int} {highest}  := subarticulations_range_upper[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[instrument1{int} {instrument1} , ks{int} {ks} , s{int} {s} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_range_upper} 
					end if
				end if
				inc(s{int} {s} ){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
		inc(ks{int} {ks} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	instrument_range[instrument1{int} {instrument1} , 0]{int} {instrument_range}  := (lowest{int} {lowest}  - range_offset_lower{int} {range_offset_lower} ) - (octave_shift[instrument1{int} {instrument1} ]{int} {octave_shift}  * 12)
	instrument_range[instrument1{int} {instrument1} , 1]{int} {instrument_range}  := (highest{int} {highest}  + range_offset_upper{int} {range_offset_upper} ) - (octave_shift[instrument1{int} {instrument1} ]{int} {octave_shift}  * 12)
end function

function update_all_ranges
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	declare local lowest : int := 128 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local highest : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}

		highest{int} {highest}  := max(highest{int} {highest} , instrument_range[i{int} {i} , 1]{int} {instrument_range} ){UserDefined, None}
		inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	nki_range[0]{int} {nki_range}  := lowest{int} {lowest} 
	nki_range[1]{int} {nki_range}  := highest{int} {highest} 
	call set_key_colors{UserDefined, None}
end function

function articulations_compute_level(ret10 : int, instrument_slot2 : int, keyswitch3 : int, note6 : int, subarticulation2 : int)
	declare local subarticulation_modulation_strength : real := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local fade_in_start : int := loaded_subarticulations_start[instrument_slot2{int} {instrument_slot2} , keyswitch3{int} {keyswitch3} , subarticulation2{int} {subarticulation2} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_start}  {Reuses: 0}
	declare local fade_in_range : int := loaded_subarticulations_fade_in[instrument_slot2{int} {instrument_slot2} , keyswitch3{int} {keyswitch3} , subarticulation2{int} {subarticulation2} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_fade_in}  {Reuses: 0}
	declare local fade_out_end : int := loaded_subarticulations_end[instrument_slot2{int} {instrument_slot2} , keyswitch3{int} {keyswitch3} , subarticulation2{int} {subarticulation2} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_end}  {Reuses: 0}
	declare local fade_out_range : int := loaded_subarticulations_fade_out[instrument_slot2{int} {instrument_slot2} , keyswitch3{int} {keyswitch3} , subarticulation2{int} {subarticulation2} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_fade_out}  {Reuses: 0}
	if(in_range(get_modulation_position(note6{int} {note6} ){UserDefined, None}, fade_in_start{int} {fade_in_start} , fade_out_end{int} {fade_out_end} ){Builtin, None})
		subarticulation_modulation_strength{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength}  := 1
		if(in_range(get_modulation_position(note6{int} {note6} ){UserDefined, None}, fade_in_start{int} {fade_in_start} , fade_in_start{int} {fade_in_start}  + fade_in_range{int} {fade_in_range} ){Builtin, None} and (fade_in_range{int} {fade_in_range}  > 0))
			subarticulation_modulation_strength{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength}  := real(get_modulation_position(note6{int} {note6} ){UserDefined, None} - fade_in_start{int} {fade_in_start} ){Builtin, None} / real(fade_in_range{int} {fade_in_range} ){Builtin, None}
		else
			if(in_range(get_modulation_position(note6{int} {note6} ){UserDefined, None}, fade_out_end{int} {fade_out_end}  - fade_out_range{int} {fade_out_range} , fade_out_end{int} {fade_out_end} ){Builtin, None} and (fade_out_range{int} {fade_out_range}  > 0))
				subarticulation_modulation_strength{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength}  := real(fade_out_end{int} {fade_out_end}  - get_modulation_position(note6{int} {note6} ){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None} / real(fade_out_range{int} {fade_out_range} ){Builtin, None}
			end if
		end if
	end if
	ret10{int} {ret10}  := int(1e+06 * ((real(articulations_compute_volume_curve(articulation_volume_min[instrument_slot2{int} {instrument_slot2} , keyswitch3{int} {keyswitch3} ]{int} {articulation_volume_min} , articulation_volume_max[instrument_slot2{int} {instrument_slot2} , keyswitch3{int} {keyswitch3} ]{int} {articulation_volume_max} , real(get_modulation_position(note6{int} {note6} ){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None} / 127, articulation_volume_curve[instrument_slot2{int} {instrument_slot2} , keyswitch3{int} {keyswitch3} ]{int} {articulation_volume_curve} ){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None} / 127) * subarticulation_modulation_strength{real} {subarticulation_modulation_strength} )){Builtin, None}
end function

function articulations_compute_volume_curve(min2 : int, max2 : int, x16 : real, curve0 : int)
	return (int(round(real(min2{int} {min2} ){Builtin, None} + (real(max2{int} {max2}  - min2{int} {min2} ){Builtin, None} * pow(x16{real} {x16} , (real(curve0{int} {curve0} ){Builtin, None} / 100) + 1){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None})
end function

function articulations_compute_modulation(instrument_slot3 : int, keyswitch4 : int, note7 : int, subarticulation3 : int, base1 : real)

function is_in_note_selection(idx16 : int, num_pressed_notes0 : int, note_selection0 : int)

		result{int} {result}  := eq(idx16{int} {idx16} , 0){UserDefined, None}
	case NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST_TWO{int} {NOTE_SELECTION_LOWEST_TWO}

function update_selected_notes

	pressed_key_idx{int} {pressed_key_idx}  := 0
	i{int} {i}  := nki_range[1]{int} {nki_range} 
	while(i{int} {i}  >= nki_range[0]{int} {nki_range} ) 
		if((pressed_keys[i{int} {i} ]{int} {pressed_keys}  > (ENGINE_UPTIME{int} {ENGINE_UPTIME}  - input_acceptance_time{int} {input_acceptance_time} )) or (((NI_CALLBACK_TYPE{int} {NI_CALLBACK_TYPE}  # NI_CB_TYPE_RELEASE{int} {NI_CB_TYPE_RELEASE} ) or (last_note_input_time{int} {last_note_input_time}  > (ENGINE_UPTIME{int} {ENGINE_UPTIME}  - input_acceptance_time{int} {input_acceptance_time} ))) and (pressed_keys[i{int} {i} ]{int} {pressed_keys}  > 0)))

				is_in_note_selection((num_pressed_keys{int} {num_pressed_keys}  - 1) - pressed_key_idx{int} {pressed_key_idx} , num_pressed_keys{int} {num_pressed_keys} , note_selections[inst{int} {inst} ]{int} {note_selections} ){UserDefined, None}
				if(is_in_note_selection_boolean{int} {is_in_note_selection_boolean}  = TRUE{int} {TRUE} )
					pressed_notes_per_instrument[inst{int} {inst} , i{int} {i} ]{int} {pressed_notes_per_instrument}  := ON{int} {ON} 
					articulations_on_note(inst{int} {inst} , i{int} {i} , max(1, key_velocity[i{int} {i} ]{int} {key_velocity} ){UserDefined, None}, pressed_keys[i{int} {i} ]{int} {pressed_keys}  - ENGINE_UPTIME{int} {ENGINE_UPTIME} ){UserDefined, None}
				else

					articulations_note_off(inst{int} {inst} , i{int} {i} ){UserDefined, None}
				end if
				inc(inst{int} {inst} ){Builtin, None}
			end while
		else
			if(pressed_keys[i{int} {i} ]{int} {pressed_keys}  > 0)
			end if
		end if

			inc(pressed_key_idx{int} {pressed_key_idx} ){Builtin, None}
		end if

	end while

	while(inst{int} {inst}  <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} {NUM_INSTRUMENTS}  - 1)) 
		active_notes[inst{int} {inst} ]{int} {active_notes}  := 0

function repetition_engine_update_tempo
	declare local new_tempo : real := real(ms_to_ticks(60000000){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None} / 960 {Reuses: 0}
	if((new_tempo{real} {new_tempo}  # tempo{real} {tempo} ) or (NI_CALLBACK_TYPE{int} {NI_CALLBACK_TYPE}  # NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER{int} {NI_CB_TYPE_LISTENER} ))
		declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
		declare local ii : int {Reuses: 0}
		declare local iii : int {Reuses: 0}
		i{int} {i}  := 0
		while(i{int} {i}  <= (NUM_INSTRUMENTS{int} {NUM_INSTRUMENTS}  - 1)) 
			ii{int} {ii}  := 0
			while(ii{int} {ii}  <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} {NUM_KEYSWITCHES}  - 1)) 
				iii{int} {iii}  := 0
				while(iii{int} {iii}  <= (NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS{int} {NUM_SUBARTICULATIONS}  - 1)) 
					if(subarticulations_type[subarticulations_ids_positions[loaded_subarticulations[i{int} {i} , ii{int} {ii} , iii{int} {iii} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations} ]{int} {subarticulations_ids_positions} ]{int} {subarticulations_type}  = SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_REPETITION{int} {SUBARTICULATION_TYPE_REPETITION} )
						repetition_interval_time[i{int} {i} , ii{int} {ii} , iii{int} {iii} ]{int} {repetition_interval_time}  := int((60000 / new_tempo{real} {new_tempo} ) * (4 / real(loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed[i{int} {i} , ii{int} {ii} , iii{int} {iii} ]{int} {loaded_subarticulations_repetition_speed} ){Builtin, None})){Builtin, None}
					end if
					inc(iii{int} {iii} ){Builtin, None}
				end while
				inc(ii{int} {ii} ){Builtin, None}
			end while
			inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
		end while
		tempo{real} {tempo}  := new_tempo{real} {new_tempo} 
	end if
end function

	end if
end function

function update_authoring_transition(start_note0 : int, end_note0 : int, dynamic_layer0 : int)

			authoring_interval_valid{int} {authoring_interval_valid}  := TRUE{int} {TRUE}

			authoring_interval_valid{int} {authoring_interval_valid}  := FALSE{int} {FALSE}

function update_authoring_labels
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_sustain_release{int} {lbl_sustain_release} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , sli_sustain_release{int} {sli_sustain_release}  & " + " & sli_sustain_release_offset{int} {sli_sustain_release_offset}  & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_trans_start{int} {lbl_trans_start} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , sli_trans_start{int} {sli_trans_start}  & " + " & sli_trans_start_offset{int} {sli_trans_start_offset}  & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_trans_fadeIn{int} {lbl_trans_fadeIn} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , int((real(sli_trans_fadeIn{int} {sli_trans_fadeIn} ){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 750){Builtin, None} & " + " & int((real(sli_trans_fadeIn_offset{int} {sli_trans_fadeIn_offset} ){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 750){Builtin, None} & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_trans_volume{int} {lbl_trans_volume} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , trim(real(sli_trans_volume{int} {sli_trans_volume} ){Builtin, None} / 1000, 2){UserDefined, None} & " + " & trim(real(sli_trans_volume_offset{int} {sli_trans_volume_offset} ){Builtin, None} / 1000, 2){UserDefined, None} & " dB"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_trans_fadeOut{int} {lbl_trans_fadeOut} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , int((real(sli_trans_fadeOut{int} {sli_trans_fadeOut} ){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 1000){Builtin, None} & " + " & int((real(sli_trans_fadeOut_offset{int} {sli_trans_fadeOut_offset} ){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 1000){Builtin, None} & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_sustain_wait{int} {lbl_sustain_wait} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , int((real(sli_sustain_wait{int} {sli_sustain_wait} ){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 500){Builtin, None} & " + " & int((real(sli_sustain_wait_offset{int} {sli_sustain_wait_offset} ){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 500){Builtin, None} & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_sustain_fadeIn{int} {lbl_sustain_fadeIn} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , int((real(sli_sustain_fadeIn{int} {sli_sustain_fadeIn} ){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 500){Builtin, None} & " + " & int((real(sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset{int} {sli_sustain_fadeIn_offset} ){Builtin, None} / 1e+06) * 500){Builtin, None} & " ms"){Builtin, None}
end function

function transition_notes_to_type(start_note1 : int, end_note1 : int)
	return (abs(end_note1{int} {end_note1}  - start_note1{int} {start_note1} ){Builtin, None} + (gt(end_note1{int} {end_note1}  - start_note1{int} {start_note1} , 0){UserDefined, None} * 12))
end function

function reset_to_main_page
	btn_main_page{int} {btn_main_page}  := ON{int} {ON} 
	btn_editor_page{int} {btn_editor_page}  := OFF{int} {OFF} 
	btn_mixer_page{int} {btn_mixer_page}  := OFF{int} {OFF} 
	call main_page_open{UserDefined, None}
	call editor_page_close{UserDefined, None}
	call mixer_page_close{UserDefined, None}
	show_keyswitches(TRUE{int} {TRUE} ){UserDefined, None}
end function

function set_background_animation(frame0 : int)
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_bg{int} {lbl_bg} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE} , "bg_ani_" & ((frame0{int} {frame0}  / 32) + 1)){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_bg{int} {lbl_bg} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_PICTURE_STATE} , min(frame0{int} {frame0}  mod 32, 30 + ne(eq(frame0{int} {frame0}  / 32, 3){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}
end function

function buffer_modwheel_animation(frame1 : int)
	next_modwheel_animation_frame{int} {next_modwheel_animation_frame}  := frame1{int} {frame1} 
end function

function set_key_colors
	declare local i : int {Reuses: 0}
	i{int} {i}  := 0
	while(i{int} {i}  <= 127) 
		set_key_color(i{int} {i} , KEY_COLOR_WHITE{int} {KEY_COLOR_WHITE} ){Builtin, None}
		if((i{int} {i}  >= nki_range[0]{int} {nki_range} ) and (i{int} {i}  <= nki_range[1]{int} {nki_range} ))
			set_key_color(i{int} {i} , KEY_COLOR_BLUE{int} {KEY_COLOR_BLUE} ){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	call keyswitches_color_keys{UserDefined, None}
end function

function main_page_close
	authoring_close{UserDefined, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_main_page{int} {pnl_main_page} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int} {HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL} ){Builtin, None}
end function

	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_main_page{int} {pnl_main_page} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} ){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_octave_layer{int} {btn_octave_layer} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , octave_layer[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} ]{int} {octave_layer} ){Builtin, None}
	mnu_note_selection{int} {mnu_note_selection}  := note_selections[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} ]{int} {note_selections} 
	mnu_transpose{int} {mnu_transpose}  := octave_shift[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} ]{int} {octave_shift} 
end function

function editor_page_open
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_editor_page{int} {pnl_editor_page} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} ){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_articulation_humanize{int} {sli_articulation_humanize} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , articulation_humanization[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} ]{int} {articulation_humanization} ){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_articulation_humanize{int} {lbl_articulation_humanize} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , sli_articulation_humanize{int} {sli_articulation_humanize}  & " ms"){Builtin, None}
	if(articulation_release[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} ]{int} {articulation_release}  >= 0)
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_articulation_release{int} {sli_articulation_release} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , articulation_release[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} ]{int} {articulation_release} ){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_articulation_release{int} {lbl_articulation_release} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , sli_articulation_release{int} {sli_articulation_release}  & " ms"){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_articulation_release_blocker{int} {btn_articulation_release_blocker} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int} {HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL} ){Builtin, None}
		btn_articulation_release{int} {btn_articulation_release}  := OFF{int} {OFF} 
	else
		set_control_par_str(get_ui_id(lbl_articulation_release{int} {lbl_articulation_release} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , ""){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_articulation_release_blocker{int} {btn_articulation_release_blocker} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} ){Builtin, None}
		btn_articulation_release{int} {btn_articulation_release}  := ON{int} {ON} 
	end if
	call update_keyswitch_volume_curve{UserDefined, None}
	call update_subarticulation_selection{UserDefined, None}
	call update_keyswitch_settings{UserDefined, None}
	call update_modwheel_assignment_circles{UserDefined, None}
	call update_modwheel_assignment_control{UserDefined, None}
	call update_dynamic_range_control{UserDefined, None}
end function

	call update_keyswitch_volume_curve{UserDefined, None}
end function

function update_keyswitch_volume_curve
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min{int} {sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_min} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , articulation_volume_min[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} ]{int} {articulation_volume_min} ){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max{int} {sli_keyswitch_volume_curve_max} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , articulation_volume_max[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} ]{int} {articulation_volume_max} ){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(sli_keyswitch_volume_curve{int} {sli_keyswitch_volume_curve} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , articulation_volume_curve[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} ]{int} {articulation_volume_curve}  * - 1){Builtin, None}
	i{int} {i}  := 0
	while(i{int} {i}  <= (num_elements[lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]} {lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope} ] - 1)) 
		set_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int} {i} ]{int} {lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope} , CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT} , articulations_compute_volume_curve(int((real(articulation_volume_min[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} ]{int} {articulation_volume_min} ){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}, int((real(articulation_volume_max[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} ]{int} {articulation_volume_max} ){Builtin, None} / 127) * 30){Builtin, None}, real(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None} / real(num_elements[lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope{int[]} {lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope} ]){Builtin, None}, articulation_volume_curve[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch} ]{int} {articulation_volume_curve} ){UserDefined, None}){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int} {i} ]{int} {lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope} , CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y{int} {CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y} , get_control_par(get_ui_id(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line{int} {lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_line} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y{int} {CONTROL_PAR_POS_Y} ){Builtin, None} - get_control_par(lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope[i{int} {i} ]{int} {lbl_keyswitch_volume_curve_envelope} , CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HEIGHT} ){Builtin, None}){Builtin, None}
		inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function center_circle_distance(ret16 : real, x17 : real, y3 : real)
	declare local dx : real := x17{real} {x17}  - 0.5 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local dy : real := y3{real} {y3}  - 0.5 {Reuses: 0}
	ret16{real} {ret16}  := sqrt((dx{real} {dx}  * dx{real} {dx} ) + (dy{real} {dy}  * dy{real} {dy} )){Builtin, None}
end function

function center_circle_angle(ret17 : real, x18 : real, y4 : real)
	declare local dx : real := x18{real} {x18}  - 0.5 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local dy : real := y4{real} {y4}  - 0.5 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local cos_theta : real := dx{real} {dx}  / sqrt((dx{real} {dx}  * dx{real} {dx} ) + (dy{real} {dy}  * dy{real} {dy} )){Builtin, None} {Reuses: 0}
	declare local angle : real := acos(cos_theta{real} {cos_theta} ){Builtin, None} {Reuses: 0}
	if(dy{real} {dy}  < 0)
		angle{real} {angle}  := (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} ) - angle{real} {angle} 
	end if
	ret17{real} {ret17}  := angle{real} {angle} 
end function

function angle_to_value(ret18 : int, angle0 : real, angle_min0 : real, angle_max0 : real)
	declare local new_angle : real := angle0{real} {angle0}  + (NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI}  / 2) {Reuses: 0}
	if(new_angle{real} {new_angle}  > (NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI}  * 2))
		new_angle{real} {new_angle}  := new_angle{real} {new_angle}  - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} )
	end if
	new_angle{real} {new_angle}  := abs(new_angle{real} {new_angle}  - (2 * NI_MATH_PI{real} {NI_MATH_PI} )){Builtin, None}
	ret18{int} {ret18}  := int((127 * (new_angle{real} {new_angle}  - angle_min0{real} {angle_min0} )) / (angle_max0{real} {angle_max0}  - angle_min0{real} {angle_min0} )){Builtin, None}
end function

				keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , i{int} {i} ]{int} {keyswitch_states}  := OFF{int} {OFF} 
				inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
			end while
		end if
		keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , idx{int} {idx} ]{int} {keyswitch_states}  := ON{int} {ON}

		call update_keyswitch_selection{UserDefined, None}
	end if
	idx{int} {idx}  := search[swi_keyswitch_purge{int[]} {swi_keyswitch_purge} , uiid3{int} {uiid3} ]

function update_keyswitch_selection
	i{int} {i}  := 0
	while(i{int} {i}  <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} {NUM_KEYSWITCHES}  - 1)) 
		set_control_par(swi_keyswitch[i{int} {i} ]{int} {swi_keyswitch} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , i{int} {i} ]{int} {keyswitch_states} ){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par_str(lbl_keyswitch[i{int} {i} ]{int} {lbl_keyswitch} , CONTROL_PAR_TEXT{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXT} , "          "){Builtin, None}
		set_control_par_str(lbl_keyswitch[i{int} {i} ]{int} {lbl_keyswitch} , CONTROL_PAR_TEXTLINE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_TEXTLINE} , "          "){Builtin, None}

		set_control_par(swi_keyswitch_purge[i{int} {i} ]{int} {swi_keyswitch_purge} , CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , keyswitch_purge_states[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , i{int} {i} ]{int} {keyswitch_purge_states} ){Builtin, None}
		set_key_pressed((keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + i{int} {i} , keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , i{int} {i} ]{int} {keyswitch_states} ){Builtin, None}
		inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
	call update_all_ranges{UserDefined, None}
	selected_subarticulation{int} {selected_subarticulation}  := 0
	if(get_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_editor_page{int} {pnl_editor_page} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} ){Builtin, None} = HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} )
		call editor_page_open{UserDefined, None}
		if(get_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_subarticulation_browser{int} {pnl_subarticulation_browser} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} ){Builtin, None} = HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} )
			call subarticulation_browser_open{UserDefined, None}
		end if
	end if
end function

function keyswitches_color_keys
	i{int} {i}  := 0
	while(i{int} {i}  <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} {NUM_KEYSWITCHES}  - 1)) 
		set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + i{int} {i} , KEY_COLOR_RED{int} {KEY_COLOR_RED} ){Builtin, None}
		if(keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , i{int} {i} ]{int} {keyswitch_states}  = ON{int} {ON} )
			set_key_color((keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + i{int} {i} , KEY_COLOR_ORANGE{int} {KEY_COLOR_ORANGE} ){Builtin, None}
		end if
		inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
	end while
end function

function keyswitches_on_note(note16 : int)
	declare local check_before : int := 0 {Reuses: 0}
	declare local changed : int := FALSE{int} {FALSE}  {Reuses: 0}
	if(in_range(note16{int} {note16} , keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12, ((keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} {NUM_KEYSWITCHES} ) - 1){Builtin, None})
		i{int} {i}  := 0
		while(i{int} {i}  <= (NUM_KEYSWITCHES{int} {NUM_KEYSWITCHES}  - 1)) 
			check_before{int} {check_before}  := keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , i{int} {i} ]{int} {keyswitch_states} 
			keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , i{int} {i} ]{int} {keyswitch_states}  := KEY_DOWN[(keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12) + i{int} {i} ]{int} {KEY_DOWN} 
			if(check_before{int} {check_before}  # keyswitch_states[selected_instrument{int} {selected_instrument} , i{int} {i} ]{int} {keyswitch_states} )
				changed{int} {changed}  := TRUE{int} {TRUE} 
			end if
			selected_keyswitch{int} {selected_keyswitch}  := note16{int} {note16}  - (keyswitch_octave{int} {keyswitch_octave}  * 12)
			inc(i{int} {i} ){Builtin, None}
		end while
		if(changed{int} {changed}  = TRUE{int} {TRUE} )
			call update_keyswitch_selection{UserDefined, None}
		end if
	end if
end function

function settings_open
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_settings{int} {pnl_settings} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_PART_NOTHING{int} {HIDE_PART_NOTHING} ){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_settings{int} {btn_settings} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , ON{int} {ON} ){Builtin, None}
end function

function settings_close
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(pnl_settings{int} {pnl_settings} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_HIDE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_HIDE} , HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL{int} {HIDE_WHOLE_CONTROL} ){Builtin, None}
	set_control_par(get_ui_id(btn_settings{int} {btn_settings} ){Builtin, None}, CONTROL_PAR_VALUE{int} {CONTROL_PAR_VALUE} , OFF{int} {OFF} ){Builtin, None}
end function
